NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

NOTICE
TATA TELESERVICES LIMITED
2,3 and 4, Paras Towers, Thiru-Vi-Ka Road, Royapettah, Chennai-600 014.
TO WHOM SO EVER IT MAY CONCERN
This is to notify that C-Forms bearing numbers TN-2005-C-AA 0514955 for a sum of Rs. 42,86,780/- and TN-2005C-AA 0514956 for a sum of Rs. 29,00,922/- issued by TATA Teleservices Limited to Messrs. Laxmi Engineers and
Contractors, Hyderabad have been reported missing. A complaint to this effect had been lodged in D2-Anna Salai Police
Station and subsequently a Non Traceable Certificate was issued vide C and O Sheet No. 75 of 2010, dated 16th March
2010 by the said Police Station.
Chennai,
6th May 2010.

Issued by TATA Teleservices Limited, Chennai,
PRAKASH, K.K.
